NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
A. MOHAMED KHAN, a male child born to M. Ameed Khan on 5th June 1964, residing at No. 28/70, Sulthan Pettai
Street, Erode-638 001, has been living as Female after an elaborate sexual reassignment Surgery by traditional
method. This has been confirmed by the Medical Board, Government Head Quarters Hospital, Erode. By this I may be
treated as a Female and shall henceforth be known as BANU.
Erode,
